class="mediawiki ltr sitedir-ltr mw-hide-empty-elt ns-0 ns-subject page-El_Ni\xc3\xb1o\xe2\x80\x93Southern_Oscillation rootpage-El_Ni\xc3\xb1o\xe2\x80\x93Southern_Oscillation class="mw-body" id="content" role="main">\n   <a id="top">\n   </a>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="siteNotice">\n    <!-- CentralNotice -->\n   </div>\n   <div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n   </div>\n   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">\n    El Ni\xc3\xb1o\xe2\x80\x93Southern Oscillation\n   </h1>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">\n     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia\n    </div>\n    <div id="contentSub">\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">\n     Jump to:\n     <a href="#mw-head">\n      navigation\n     </a>\n     ,\n     <a href="#p-search">\n      search\n     </a>\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">\n     <div class="mw-parser-output">\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Soi.svg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1000" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Soi.svg/220px-Soi.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Soi.svg/330px-Soi.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Soi.svg/440px-Soi.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Soi.svg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Southern Oscillation Index timeseries 1876\xe2\x80\x932012.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        El Ni\xc3\xb1o\xe2\x80\x93Southern Oscillation\n       </b>\n       (\n       <i>\n        ENSO\n       </i>\n       ) is an irregularly periodic variation in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Winds" title="Winds">\n        winds\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        sea surface temperatures\n       </a>\n       over the tropical eastern Pacific Ocean, affecting much of the tropics and subtropics. The warming phase is known as\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/El_Ni%C3%B1o" title="El Ni\xc3\xb1o">\n         El Ni\xc3\xb1o\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       and the cooling phase as\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/La_Ni%C3%B1a" title="La Ni\xc3\xb1a">\n         La Ni\xc3\xb1a\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       .\n       <i>\n        Southern Oscillation\n       </i>\n       is the accompanying atmospheric component, coupled with the sea temperature change:\n       <i>\n        El Ni\xc3\xb1o\n       </i>\n       is accompanied with high, and\n       <i>\n        La Ni\xc3\xb1a\n       </i>\n       with low air\n       <a href="/wiki/Surface_pressure" title="Surface pressure">\n        surface pressure\n       </a>\n       in the tropical western Pacific.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPC_ENSO_1-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPC_ENSO-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The two periods last several months each (typically occurring every few years) and their effects vary in intensity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The two phases relate to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Walker_circulation" title="Walker circulation">\n        Walker circulation\n       </a>\n       , discovered by\n       <a href="/wiki/Gilbert_Walker" title="Gilbert Walker">\n        Gilbert Walker\n       </a>\n       during the early twentieth century. The Walker circulation is caused by the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pressure_gradient_force" title="Pressure gradient force">\n        pressure gradient force\n       </a>\n       that results from a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/High_pressure_area" title="High pressure area">\n        high pressure system\n       </a>\n       over the eastern Pacific Ocean, and a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_system" title="Low pressure system">\n        low pressure system\n       </a>\n       over\n       <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">\n        Indonesia\n       </a>\n       . When the Walker circulation weakens or reverses, an\n       <i>\n        El Ni\xc3\xb1o\n       </i>\n       results, causing the ocean surface to be warmer than average, as upwelling of cold water occurs less or not at all. An especially strong Walker circulation causes a\n       <i>\n        La Ni\xc3\xb1a\n       </i>\n       , resulting in cooler ocean temperatures due to increased upwelling.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Mechanisms that cause the oscillation remain under study. The extremes of this climate pattern\'s oscillations cause extreme weather (such as floods and droughts) in many regions of the world. Developing countries dependent upon agriculture and fishing, particularly those bordering the Pacific Ocean, are the most affected.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n         <a href="#Concept">\n </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-3">\n         <a href="#Sea_surface_temperature_oscillation">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           3\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Sea surface temperature oscillation\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-4">\n           <a href="#Neutral_phase">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Neutral phase\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-5">\n           <a href="#Warm_phase">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             3.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Cold phase\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li         <span class="tocnumber">\n           4\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Southern Oscillation\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-9">\n         <a href="#Madden.E2.80.93Julian_oscillation">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           5\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Madden\xe2\x80\x93Julian oscillation\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-10">\n         <a href="#Impacts">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           6\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Impacts\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-11">\n           <a href="#On_precipitation">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             6.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             On precipitation\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-12">\n           <a href="#On_Tehuantepecers">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             6.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             On Tehuantepecers\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-13">\n           <a href="#On_global_warming">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             6.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             On global warming\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-14">\n           <a href="#On_coral_bleaching">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n        </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-16">\n         <a href="#Diversity">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-18">\n         <a href="#References">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           9\n          </span>\n          <span
